## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Input: operationType] --> B{operationType in map?}
    B -- CREATE --> C["label: Created\ncolor: success"]
    B -- UPDATE --> D["label: Updated\ncolor: info"]
    B -- DELETE --> E["label: Deleted\ncolor: danger"]
    B -- ASSIGN_WORKSPACE --> F["label: Workspace Assigned\ncolor: success"]
    B -- UNASSIGN_WORKSPACE --> G["label: Workspace Unassigned\ncolor: warning"]
    B -- ADD_ORG_PERMISSION --> H["label: Organization Permission Added\ncolor: success"]
    B -- UPDATE_ORG_PERMISSION --> I["label: Organization Permission Updated\ncolor: info"]
    B -- REMOVE_ORG_PERMISSION --> J["label: Organization Permission Removed\ncolor: danger"]
    B -- not_found --> K["return operationType or 'secondary' for color"]
    subgraph Mapping
        C & D & E & F & G & H & I & J
    end
    C --> L[Output: formatted label]
    D --> L
    E --> L
    F --> L
    G --> L
    H --> L
    I --> L
    J --> L
    K --> L
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant U as useAuditLogFormatters
    participant T as i18n t
    participant C as Caller
    C->>U: formatEntityType("REPORT")
    U->>T: t("admin-reports:Report")
    T-->>U: "Report"
    U-->>C: "Report"
    C->>U: formatActorId("auth|user@example.com")
    U->>U: split by "|"
    U-->>C: "user@example.com"
    C->>getOperationBadgeColor: getOperationBadgeColor(UPDATE)
    getOperationBadgeColor-->>C: "info"
```
